\\gamma \\text{ (lr)}, \\: \\theta_0 \\text{ (params)}, \\: f(\\theta)\n                \\text{ (objective)}, \\: \\lambda \\text{ (weight decay)},                          \\\\\n                                               \\\\[-1.ex]\n       \\end{aligned}\n\n    Nesterov momentum is based on the formula from\n    `On the importance of initialization and momentum in deep learning`__.\n    \"\"\"\n    + rf\"\"\"\n    Args:\n        {_params_doc}\n        lr (float, Tensor, optional): learning rate (default: 1e-3)\n        momentum (float, optional): momentum factor This is in contrast to some other\n        frameworks that initialize it to all zeros. One notable side effect\n        of this decision is that the first momentum value will not be scaled\n        by dampening. Dampening will be applied starting at the second step.\n\n    \"\"\"\n)\n\n\ndef sgd(\n    params: list[Tensor],\n    d_p_list: list[Tensor],\n    momentum_buffer_list: list[Optional[Tensor]],\n    # kwonly args with defaults are not supported by functions compiled with torchscript issue #70627\n    # setting this as kwarg for now as functional API is compiled by torch/distributed/optim\n    has_sparse_grad: bool = False,\n    foreach: Optional[bool] = None,\n    fused: Optional[bool] = None,\n    grad_scale: Optional[Tensor] = None,\n    found_inf: Optional[Tensor] = None,\n    *,\n    weight_decay: float,\n    momentum: float,\n    lr: float,\n    dampening: float,\n    nesterov: bool,\n    maximize: bool,\n):\n    r\"\"\"Functional API that performs SGD algorithm computation.\n\n    See :class:`~torch.optim.SGD` for details.\n    \"\"\"\n    # Respect when the user inputs False/True for foreach or fused.        )\n   404→\n   405→        # update step\n   406→        step_t += 1\n   407→\n   408→        if weight_decay != 0:\n   409→            if decoupled_weight_decay:\n   410→                # Perform stepweight decay\n   411→                param.mul_(1 - lr * weight_decay)\n   412→            else:\n   413→                # Nested if is necessary to bypass jitscript rules\n   414→                if differentiable and isinstance(weight_decay, Tensor):\n   415→                    if weight_decay.requires_grad:\n   416→                        grad = grad.addcmul_(param.clone(), weight_decay)\n   417→                    else:\n   418→                        grad = grad.add(param, alpha=weight_decay)\n   419→                else:\n   420→                    grad = grad.add(param, alpha=weight_decay)\n   421→\n   422→        if torch.is_complex(param):\n   423→            grad = torch.view_as_real(grad)\n   424→            exp_avg = torch.view_as_real(exp_avg)\n   425→            exp_avg_sq = torch.view_as_real(exp_avg_sq)\n   426→            if amsgrad:\n   427→                max_exp_avg_sqs[i] = torch.view_as_real(max_exp_avg_sqs[i])\n   428→            param = torch.view_as_real(param)\n   429→\n   430→        device = param.device\n   431→\n   432→        if beta1_dict is not None:\n   433→            dtype = param.dtype  # type: ignore[union-attr]\n   434→\n   435→            # cast to workaround https://github.com/pytorch/pytorch/issues/140601\n   436→            key = (device, dtype)\n   437→            if key not in beta1_dict:\n   438→                beta1_dict[key] = beta1.to(  # type: ignore[union-attr]\n   439→                    device=device, dtype=dtype, non_blocking=True\n   440→                )\n   441→\n   442→            device_beta1: Union[float, Tensor] = beta1_dict[key]\n   443→        else:\n   444→            device_beta1 = beta1\n   445→\n   446→        # Decay the first and second moment running average coefficient\n   447→        exp_avg.lerp_(grad, 1 - device_beta1)\n   448→\n   449→        # Nested if is necessary to bypass jitscript rules\n   450→        if differentiable and isinstance(beta2, Tensor):\n   451→            if beta2.requires_grad:\n   452→                # Using lerp to only use 2 operations bc addcmul's value cannot be a tensor\n   453→                # Showing equivalence of differentiable path and nondifferentiable path\n   454→                # expavg * b2 + grad^2 * (1-b2)\n   455→                #           add expavg * (1-b2) - expavg * (1-b2) = 0\n   456→                # expavg * b2 + expavg * (1-b2) - expavg * (1-b2) + grad^2 * (1-b2)\n   457→                # expavg - expavg * (1-b2) + grad^2 * (1-b2)\n   458→                # expavg + (grad^2 - expavg) * (1-b2)\n   459→                # expavg.lerp(grad^2, 1-beta2)\n   460→                exp_avg_sq.lerp_(torch.square(grad), weight=1 - beta2)\n   461→            else:\n   462→                exp_avg_sq.mul_(beta2).addcmul_(\n   463→                    grad, grad, value=cast(float, 1 - beta2)\n   464→                )\n   465→        else:\n   466→            exp_avg_sq.mul_(beta2).addcmul_(grad, grad, value=1 - beta2)  # type: ignore[arg-type]\n   467→\n   468→        if capturable or differentiable:\n   469→            step = step_t\n   470→\n   471→            # Nested if is necessary to bypass jitscript rules\n   472→            if differentiable and isinstance(beta1, Tensor):\n   473→                if beta1.requires_grad:\n   474→                    bias_correction1 = 1 - beta1 ** step.clone()\n   475→                else:\n   476→                    bias_correction1 = 1 - beta1**step\n   477→            else:\n   478→                bias_correction1 = 1 - beta1**step\n   479→\n   480→            # Nested if is necessary to bypass jitscript rules\n   481→            if differentiable and isinstance(beta2, Tensor):\n   482→                if beta2.requires_grad:\n   483→                    bias_correction2 = 1 - beta2 ** step.clone()\n   484→                else:\n   485→                    bias_correction2 = 1 - beta2**step\n   486→            else:\n   487→                bias_correction2 = 1 - beta2**step\n   488→\n   489→            step_size = lr / bias_correction1\n   490→            step_size_neg = step_size.neg()\n   491→\n   492→            bias_correction2_sqrt = bias_correction2.sqrt()\n   493→\n   494→            if amsgrad:\n   495→                # Maintains the maximum of all 2nd moment running avg. till now\n   496→                if differentiable:\n   497→                    max_exp_avg_sq = max_exp_avg_sqs[i].clone()\n   498→                else:\n   499→                    max_exp_avg_sq = max_exp_avg_sqs[i]\n   500→\n   501→                max_exp_avg_sqs[i].copy_(torch.maximum(max_exp_avg_sq, exp_avg_sq))\n   502→\n   503→                # Uses the max. for normalizing running avg. of gradient\n   504→                # Folds in (admittedly ugly) 1-elem step_size math here to avoid extra param-set-sized read+write\n   505→                # (can't fold it into addcdiv_ below because addcdiv_ requires value is a Number, not a Tensor)\n   506→                denom = (\n   507→                    max_exp_avg_sqs[i].sqrt() / (bias_correction2_sqrt * step_size_neg)\n   508→                ).add_(eps / step_size_neg)\n   509→            else:\n   510→                denom = (\n   511→                    exp_avg_sq.sqrt() / (bias_correction2_sqrt * step_size_neg)\n   512→                ).add_(eps / step_size_neg)\n   513→\n   514→            if differentiable:\n   515→                param.addcdiv_(exp_avg.clone(), denom)\n   516→            else:\n   517→                param.addcdiv_(exp_avg, denom)\n   518→        else:\n   519→            step = _get_value(step_t)\n   520→\n   521→            bias_correction1 = 1 - beta1**step\n   522→            bias_correction2 = 1 - beta2**step\n   523→\n   524→            step_size = lr / bias_correction1\n   525→\n   526→            bias_correction2_sqrt = bias_correction2**0.5\n   527→\n   528→            if amsgrad:\n   529→                # Maintains the maximum of all 2nd moment running avg. till now\n   530→                torch.maximum(max_exp_avg_sqs[i], exp_avg_sq, out=max_exp_avg_sqs[i])\n   531→\n   532→                # Use the max. for normalizing running avg. of gradient\n   533→                denom = (max_exp_avg_sqs[i].sqrt() / bias_correction2_sqrt).add_(eps)\n   534→            else:\n   535→                denom = (exp_avg_sq.sqrt() / bias_correction2_sqrt).add_(eps)\n   536→\n   537→            param.addcdiv_(exp_avg, denom, value=-step_size)  # type: ignore[arg-type]\n   538→\n   539→        # Lastly, switch back to complex view\n   540→        if amsgrad and torch.is_complex(params[i]):\n   541→            max_exp_avg_sqs[i] = torch.view_as_complex(max_exp_avg_sqs[i])\n   542→\n   543→\n   544→def _multi_tensor_adam(\n   545→    params: list[Tensor],\n   546→    grads: list[Tensor],\n   547→    exp_avgs: list[Tensor],\n   548→    exp_avg_sqs: list[Tensor],\n   549→    max_exp_avg_sqs: list[Tensor],\n   550→    state_steps: list[Tensor],\n   551→    grad_scale: Optional[Tensor],\n   552→    found_inf: Optional[Tensor],\n   553→    *,\n   554→    amsgrad: bool,\n   555→    has_complex: bool,\n   556→    beta1: Union[float, Tensor],\n   557→    beta2: Union[float, Tensor],\n   558→    lr: Union[float, Tensor],\n   559→    weight_decay: float,\n   560→    eps: float,\n   561→    maximize: bool,\n   562→    capturable: bool,\n   563→    differentiable: bool,\n   564→    decoupled_weight_decay: bool,\n   565→):\n   566→    if len(params) == 0:\n   567→        return\n   568→\n   569→    if isinstance(lr, Tensor):\n   570→        if not capturable:\n   571→            raise RuntimeError(\n   572→                \"lr as a Tensor is not supported for capturable=False and foreach=True\"\n   573→            )\n   574→        if lr.numel() != 1:\n   575→            raise ValueError(\"Tensor lr must be 1-element\")\n   576→\n   577→    if isinstance(beta1, Tensor):\n   578→        if not capturable:\n   579→            raise ValueError(\n   580→                \"beta1 as a Tensor is not supported for capturable=False and foreach=True\"\n   581→            )\n   582→        if beta1.numel() != 1:\n   583→            raise ValueError(\"Tensor beta1 must be 1-element\")\n   584→\n   585→    if isinstance(beta2, Tensor):\n   586→        if not capturable:\n   587→            raise ValueError(\n   588→                \"beta2 as a Tensor is not supported for capturable=False and foreach=True\"\n   589→            )\n   590→        if beta2.numel() != 1:\n   591→            raise ValueError(\"Tensor beta2 must be 1-element\")\n   592→\n   593→    # If compiling, the compiler will handle cudagraph checks, see note [torch.compile x capturable]\n   594→    if not torch.compiler.is_compiling() and capturable:\n   595→        capturable_supported_devices = _get_capturable_supported_devices(\n   596→            supports_xla=False\n   597→        )\n   598→        assert all(\n   599→            p.device.type == step.device.type\n   600→            and p.device.type in capturable_supported_devices\n   601→            for p, step in zip(params, state_steps)\n   602→        ), (\n   603→            f\"If capturable=True, params and state_steps must be on supported devices: {capturable_supported_devices}.\"\n   604→        )\n   605→\n   606→    assert grad_scale is None and found_inf is None\n   607→\n   608→    assert not differentiable, \"_foreach ops don't support autograd\"\n   609→\n   610→    lr = _to_scalar(lr)\n   611→    # TODO: Support nonzero-dim Tensor betas, see #147921\n   612→\n   613→    grouped_tensors = Optimizer._group_tensors_by_device_and_dtype(\n   614→        [params, grads, exp_avgs, exp_avg_sqs, max_exp_avg_sqs, state_steps]  # type: ignore[list-item]\n   615→    )\n   616→\n   617→    # We only shuffle around the beta when it is a Tensor and on CUDA, otherwise, we prefer\n   618→    # treating it as a scalar.\n   619→    beta1_dict: Optional[DeviceDict] = (  # type: ignore[attr-defined]\n   620→        {beta1.device: beta1}\n   621→        if isinstance(beta1, Tensor) and str(beta1.device) != \"cpu\"\n   622→        else None\n   623→    )\n   624→\n   625→    for (\n   626→        device_params_,\n   627→        device_grads_,\n   628→        device_exp_avgs_,\n   629→        device_exp_avg_sqs_,\n   630→        device_max_exp_avg_sqs_,\n   631→        device_state_steps_,\n   632→    ), _ in grouped_tensors.values():\n   633→        device_params = cast(list[Tensor], device_params_)\n   634→        device_grads = cast(list[Tensor], device_grads_)\n   635→        device_exp_avgs = cast(list[Tensor], device_exp_avgs_)\n   636→        device_exp_avg_sqs = cast(list[Tensor], device_exp_avg_sqs_)\n   637→        device_state_steps = cast(list[Tensor], device_state_steps_)\n   638→\n   639→        device = device_params[0].device\n   640→        if beta1_dict is not None and device not in beta1_dict:\n   641→            beta1_dict[device] = beta1.to(device=device, non_blocking=True)  # type: ignore[union-attr, attr-defined]\n   642→\n   643→        device_beta1 = beta1_dict[device] if beta1_dict else beta1\n   644→\n   645→        # Handle complex parameters\n   646→        if has_complex:\n   647→            if amsgrad:\n   648→                device_max_exp_avg_sqs = cast(list[Tensor], device_max_exp_avg_sqs_)\n   649→                _view_as_real(\n   650→                    device_params,\n   651→                    device_grads,\n   652→                    device_exp_avgs,\n   653→                    device_exp_avg_sqs,\n   654→                    device_max_exp_avg_sqs,\n   655→                )\n   656→            else:\n   657→                _view_as_real(\n   658→                    device_params, device_grads, device_exp_avgs, device_exp_avg_sqs\n   659→                )\n   660→\n   661→        if maximize:\n   662→            device_grads = torch._foreach_neg(device_grads)  # type: ignore[assignment]\n   663→\n   664→        # Update steps\n   665→        # If steps are on CPU, foreach will fall back to the slow path, which is a for-loop calling t.add(1) over\n   666→        # and over. 1 will then be wrapped into a Tensor over and over again, which is slower than if we just\n   667→        # wrapped it once now. The alpha is required to assure we go to the right overload.\n   668→        if not torch.compiler.is_compiling() and device_state_steps[0].is_cpu:\n   669→            torch._foreach_add_(\n   670→                device_state_steps, torch.tensor(1.0, device=\"cpu\"), alpha=1.0\n   671→            )\n   672→        else:\n   673→            torch._foreach_add_(device_state_steps, 1)\n   674→\n   675→        if weight_decay != 0:\n   676→            if decoupled_weight_decay:\n   677→                # Perform stepweight decay\n   678→                torch._foreach_mul_(device_params, 1 - lr * weight_decay)\n   679→            else:\n   680→                # Reuse the intermediate memory (device_grads) already allocated for maximize\n   681→                if maximize:\n   682→                    torch._foreach_add_(device_grads, device_params, alpha=weight_decay)\n   683→                else:\n   684→                    device_grads = torch._foreach_add(  # type: ignore[assignment]\n   685→                        device_grads, device_params, alpha=weight_decay\n   686→                    )\n   687→\n   688→        # Decay the first and second moment running average coefficient\n   689→        # Use device beta1 if beta1 is a tensor to ensure all\n   690→        # tensors are on the same device\n   691→        torch._foreach_lerp_(\n   692→            device_exp_avgs, device_grads, cast(float, 1 - device_beta1)\n   693→        )\n   694→\n   695→        torch._foreach_mul_(device_exp_avg_sqs, beta2)\n   696→\n   697→        # Due to the strictness of the _foreach_addcmul API, we can't have a single\n   698→        # tensor scalar as the scalar arg (only python number is supported there)\n   699→        # as a result, separate out the value mul\n   700→        # Filed https://github.com/pytorch/pytorch/issues/139795\n   701→        if isinstance(beta2, torch.Tensor):\n   702→            scaled_device_grads = torch._foreach_mul(device_grads, 1 - beta2)  # type: ignore[assignment]\n   703→            value = 1.0\n   704→        else:\n   705→            scaled_device_grads = device_grads  # type: ignore[assignment]\n   706→            value = 1 - beta2\n   707→\n   708→        torch._foreach_addcmul_(\n   709→            device_exp_avg_sqs, scaled_device_grads, device_grads, value\n   710→        )\n   711→\n   712→        # Delete the local intermediate(s) since they won't be used anymore to save on peak memory\n   713→        del device_grads\n   714→        del scaled_device_grads\n   715→\n   716→        bias_correction1: Union[tuple[Tensor, ...], list[Tensor]]\n   717→        bias_correction2: Union[tuple[Tensor, ...], list[Tensor]]\n   718→        bias_correction2_sqrt: Union[tuple[Tensor, ...], list[Tensor]]\n   719→\n   720→        if capturable:\n   721→            bias_correction1 = torch._foreach_pow(beta1, device_state_steps)  # type: ignore[arg-type]\n   722→            bias_correction2 = torch._foreach_pow(beta2, device_state_steps)  # type: ignore[arg-type]\n   723→            # foreach_sub doesn't allow a scalar as the first arg\n   724→            torch._foreach_sub_(bias_correction1, 1)\n   725→            torch._foreach_sub_(bias_correction2, 1)\n   726→            # we do not negate bias_correction1 as it'll need to be negated later anyway\n   727→            torch._foreach_neg_(bias_correction2)\n   728→\n   729→            # foreach_div doesn't allow a scalar as the first arg\n   730→            torch._foreach_div_(bias_correction1, lr)\n   731→            torch._foreach_reciprocal_(bias_correction1)\n   732→\n   733→            torch._foreach_sqrt_(bias_correction2)\n   734→\n   735→            # Re-assign for clarity as we maintain minimal intermediates: we'll have\n   736→            # step_size = - lr / (1 - beta1 ^ t) where t = num_steps\n   737→            # bias_correction2_sqrt = sqrt(1 - beta2 ^ t)\n   738→            step_size = bias_correction1\n   739→            bias_correction2_sqrt = bias_correction2\n   740→\n   741→            if amsgrad:\n   742→                device_max_exp_avg_sqs = cast(list[Tensor], device_max_exp_avg_sqs_)\n   743→                # Maintains the maximum of all 2nd moment running avg. till now\n   744→                torch._foreach_maximum_(device_max_exp_avg_sqs, device_exp_avg_sqs)  # type: ignore[assignment]\n   745→\n   746→                # Set intermediate to the max. for normalizing running avg. of gradient when amsgrad\n   747→                exp_avg_sq_sqrt = torch._foreach_sqrt(device_max_exp_avg_sqs)\n   748→            else:\n   749→                exp_avg_sq_sqrt = torch._foreach_sqrt(device_exp_avg_sqs)\n   750→\n   751→            torch._foreach_div_(exp_avg_sq_sqrt, bias_correction2_sqrt)\n   752→            torch._foreach_add_(exp_avg_sq_sqrt, eps)\n   753→            torch._foreach_div_(exp_avg_sq_sqrt, step_size)\n   754→\n   755→            # at this point, exp_avg_sq_sqrt = - (1 - beta^t) * [sqrt(exp_avg_sq / (1 - beta2^t)) + eps] / lr\n   756→            torch._foreach_addcdiv_(device_params, device_exp_avgs, exp_avg_sq_sqrt)\n   757→        else:\n   758→            bias_correction1 = [\n   759→                1 - beta1 ** _get_value(step) for step in device_state_steps\n   760→            ]\n   761→            bias_correction2 = [\n   762→                1 - beta2 ** _get_value(step) for step in device_state_steps\n   763→            ]\n   764→\n   765→            step_size = _stack_if_compiling([(lr / bc) * -1 for bc in bias_correction1])\n   766→\n   767→            bias_correction2_sqrt = [bc**0.5 for bc in bias_correction2]  # type: ignore[arg-type]\n   768→\n   769→            if amsgrad:\n   770→                device_max_exp_avg_sqs = cast(list[Tensor], device_max_exp_avg_sqs_)\n   771→                # Maintains the maximum of all 2nd moment running avg. till now\n   772→                torch._foreach_maximum_(device_max_exp_avg_sqs, device_exp_avg_sqs)\n   773→\n   774→                # Use the max. for normalizing running avg. of gradient\n   775→                exp_avg_sq_sqrt = torch._foreach_sqrt(device_max_exp_avg_sqs)\n   776→            else:\n   777→                exp_avg_sq_sqrt = torch._foreach_sqrt(device_exp_avg_sqs)\n   778→\n   779→            torch._foreach_div_(exp_avg_sq_sqrt, bias_correction2_sqrt)\n   780→            torch._foreach_add_(exp_avg_sq_sqrt, eps)\n   781→            torch._foreach_addcdiv_(\n   782→                device_params,\n   783→                device_exp_avgs,\n   784→                exp_avg_sq_sqrt,\n   785→                step_size,  # type: ignore[arg-type]\n   786→            )\n   787→\n   788→\n   789→def _fused_adam(\n   790→    params: list[Tensor],\n   791→    grads: list[Tensor],\n   792→    exp_avgs: list[Tensor],\n   793→    exp_avg_sqs: list[Tensor],\n   794→    max_exp_avg_sqs: list[Tensor],\n   795→    state_steps: list[Tensor],\n   796→    grad_scale: Optional[Tensor],\n   797→    found_inf: Optional[Tensor],\n   798→    *,\n   799→    amsgrad: bool,\n   800→    has_complex: bool,  # Needed for consistency.\n   801→    beta1: float,\n   802→    beta2: float,\n   803→    lr: Union[float, Tensor],\n   804→    weight_decay: float,\n   805→    eps: float,\n   806→    maximize: bool,\n   807→    capturable: bool,  # Needed for consistency.\n   808→    differentiable: bool,\n   809→    decoupled_weight_decay: bool,\n   810→) -> None:\n   811→    if not params:\n   812→        return\n   813→    if differentiable:\n   814→        raise RuntimeError(\"Adam with fused=True does not support differentiable=True\")\n   815→\n   816→    grad_scale_dict: DeviceDict = (\n   817→        {grad_scale.device: grad_scale} if grad_scale is not None else {}\n   818→    )\n   819→    found_inf_dict: DeviceDict = (\n   820→        {found_inf.device: found_inf} if found_inf is not None else {}\n   821→    )\n   822→\n   823→    # We only shuffle around the lr when it is a Tensor and on CUDA, otherwise, we prefer\n   824→    # treating it as a scalar.\n   825→    lr_dict: Optional[DeviceDict] = (\n   826→        {lr.device: lr} if isinstance(lr, Tensor) and str(lr.device) != \"cpu\" else None\n   827→    )\n   828→    grouped_tensors = Optimizer._group_tensors_by_device_and_dtype(\n   829→        [params, grads, exp_avgs, exp_avg_sqs, max_exp_avg_sqs, state_steps]  # type: ignore[list-item]\n   830→    )\n   831→    for (device, _), (\n   832→        (\n   833→            device_params_,\n   834→            device_grads_,\n   835→            device_exp_avgs_,\n   836→            device_exp_avg_sqs_,\n   837→            device_max_exp_avg_sqs,\n   838→            device_state_steps_,\n   839→        ),\n   840→        _,\n   841→    ) in grouped_tensors.items():\n   842→        device_params = cast(list[Tensor], device_params_)\n   843→        device_grads = cast(list[Tensor], device_grads_)\n   844→        device_exp_avgs = cast(list[Tensor], device_exp_avgs_)\n   845→        device_exp_avg_sqs = cast(list[Tensor], device_exp_avg_sqs_)\n   846→        device_state_steps = cast(list[Tensor], device_state_steps_)\n   847→\n   848→        device_grad_scale, device_found_inf = None, None\n   849→        if grad_scale is not None:\n   850→            device_grad_scale = grad_scale_dict.setdefault(\n   851→                device, grad_scale.to(device, non_blocking=True)\n   852→            )\n   853→        if found_inf is not None:\n   854→            device_found_inf = found_inf_dict.setdefault(\n   855→                device, found_inf.to(device, non_blocking=True)\n   856→            )\n   857→        if lr_dict is not None and device not in lr_dict:\n   858→            lr_dict[device] = lr.to(device=device, non_blocking=True)  # type: ignore[union-attr]\n   859→            lr = lr_dict[device]\n   860→        torch._foreach_add_(device_state_steps, 1)\n   861→        func = torch._fused_adam_ if not decoupled_weight_decay else torch._fused_adamw_\n   862→        func(\n   863→            device_params,\n   864→            device_grads,\n   865→            device_exp_avgs,\n   866→            device_exp_avg_sqs,\n   867→            device_max_exp_avg_sqs,  # type: ignore[arg-type]\n   868→            device_state_steps,\n   869→            amsgrad=amsgrad,\n   870→            lr=lr,  # type: ignore[arg-type]\n   871→            beta1=beta1,\n   872→            beta2=beta2,\n   873→            weight_decay=weight_decay,\n   874→            eps=eps,\n   875→            maximize=maximize,\n   876→            grad_scale=device_grad_scale,\n   877→            found_inf=device_found_inf,\n   878→        )\n   879→        if device_found_inf is not None:\n   880→            torch._foreach_sub_(\n   881→                device_state_steps, [device_found_inf] * len(device_state_steps)\n   882→            )\n   883→\n   884→\n   885→@_disable_dynamo_if_unsupported(single_tensor_fn=_single_tensor_adam)\n   886→def adam(\n   887→    params: list[Tensor],\n   888→    grads: list[Tensor],\n   889→    exp_avgs: list[Tensor],\n   890→    exp_avg_sqs: list[Tensor],\n   891→    max_exp_avg_sqs: list[Tensor],\n   892→    state_steps: list[Tensor],\n   893→    # r\"\"\"Implements Adam algorithm.\n\n    .. math::\n       \\begin{aligned}\n            &\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                                 \\\\\n            &\\textbf{input}      : \\gamma \\text{ (lr)}, \\beta_1, \\beta_2\n                \\text{ (betas)},\\theta_0 \\text{ (params)},f(\\theta) \\text{ (objective)}          \\\\\n            &\\hspace{13mm}      \\lambda \\text{ (weight decay)},  \\: \\textit{amsgrad},\n                \\:\\textit{maximize},  \\: \\epsilon \\text{ (epsilon)}                              \\\\\n            &\\textbf{initialize} :  m_0 \\leftarrow 0 \\text{ ( first moment)},\n                v_0\\leftarrow 0 \\text{ (second moment)},\\: v_0^{max}\\leftarrow 0          \\\\[-1.ex]\n            &\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                                 \\\\\n            &\\textbf{for} \\: t=1 \\: \\textbf{to} \\: \\ldots \\: \\textbf{do}                         \\\\\n\n            &\\hspace{5mm}\\textbf{if} \\: \\textit{maximize}:                                       \\\\\n            &\\hspace{10mm}g_t           \\leftarrow   -\\nabla_{\\theta} f_t (\\theta_{t-1})         \\\\\n            &\\hspace{5mm}\\textbf{else}                                                           \\\\\n            &\\hspace{10mm}g_t           \\leftarrow   \\nabla_{\\theta} f_t (\\theta_{t-1})          \\\\\n            &\\hspace{5mm}\\textbf{if} \\: \\lambda \\neq 0                                           \\\\\n            &\\hspace{10mm} g_t \\leftarrow g_t + \\lambda  \\theta_{t-1}                            \\\\\n            &\\hspace{5mm}m_t           \\leftarrow   \\beta_1 m_{t-1} + (1 - \\beta_1) g_t          \\\\\n            &\\hspace{5mm}v_t           \\leftarrow   \\beta_2 v_{t-1} + (1-\\beta_2) g^2_t          \\\\\n            &\\hspace{5mm}\\widehat{m_t} \\leftarrow   m_t/\\big(1-\\beta_1^t \\big)                   \\\\\n            &\\hspace{5mm}\\textbf{if} \\: amsgrad                                                  \\\\\n            &\\hspace{10mm} v_t^{max} \\leftarrow \\mathrm{max}(v_{t-1}^{max},v_t)                  \\\\\n            &\\hspace{10mm}\\widehat{v_t} \\leftarrow v_t^{max}/\\big(1-\\beta_2^t \\big)              \\\\\n            &\\hspace{5mm}\\textbf{else}                                                           \\\\\n            &\\hspace{10mm}\\widehat{v_t} \\leftarrow   v_t/\\big(1-\\beta_2^t \\big)                  \\\\\n            &\\hspace{5mm}\\theta_t \\leftarrow \\theta_{t-1} - \\gamma \\widehat{m_t}/\n                \\big(\\sqrt{\\widehat{v_t}} + \\epsilon \\big)                                       \\\\\n            &\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                          \\\\[-1.ex]\n            &\\bf{return} \\:  \\theta_t                                                     \\\\[-1.ex]\n            &\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                          \\\\[-1.ex]\n       \\end{aligned}\n\n    For further details regarding the algorithm we refer to `Adam: A Method for Stochastic Optimization`_.\n    \"\"\"\n    + rf\"\"\"\n    Args:\n        {_params_doc}\n        lr (float, Tensor, optional): learning rate (default: 1e-3). A tensor LR\n            is not yet supported for all our implementations. Please use a float\n            LR if you are not also specifying fused=True or capturable=True.\n        betas (Tuple[float, float], optional): coefficients used for computing\n            running averages of gradient and its square (default: (0.9, 0.999))\n        eps (float, optional): term added to the denominator to improve\n            numerical stability (default: 1e-8)\n        weight_decay (float, optional): weight decay (L2 penalty) (default: 0)\n        decoupled_weight_decay (bool, optional): if True, this optimizer is\n            equivalent to AdamW and the algorithm will not accumulate weight\n            decay in the momentum nor variance. (default: False)\n        amsgrad (bool, optional): whether to use the AMSGrad variant of this\n            algorithm from the paper `On the Convergence of Adam and Beyond`_\n            (default: False)\n        {_foreach_doc}\n        {_maximize_doc}\n        {_capturable_doc}\n        {_differentiable_doc}\n        {_fused_doc}\n    .. Note::\n        A prototype implementation of Adam and AdamW for MPS supports `torch.float32` and `torch.float16`.\n    .. _Adam\\: A Method for Stochastic Optimization:\n        https://arxiv.org/abs/1412.6980\n    .. _On the Convergence of Adam and Beyond:\n        https://openreview.net/forum?id=ryQu7f-RZ\n\n    \"\"\"\n)\n\n\ndef _single_tensor_adam(\n    params: list[Tensor],\n    grads: list[Tensor],\n    exp_avgs: list[Tensor],\n    exp_avg_sqs: list[Tensor],\n    max_exp_avg_sqs: list[Tensor],\n    state_steps: list[Tensor],\n    grad_scale: Optional[Tensor],\n    found_inf: Optional[Tensor],\n    *,\n    amsgrad: bool,\n    has_complex: bool,\n    beta1: Union[float, Tensor],\n    beta2: Union[float, Tensor],\n    lr: Union[float, Tensor],\n    weight_decay: float,\n    eps: float,\n    maximize: bool,\n    capturable: bool,\n    differentiable: bool,\n    decoupled_weight_decay: bool,\n):\n    assert grad_scale is None and found_inf is None\n\n    if torch.jit.is_scripting():\n        # this assert is due to JIT being dumb and not realizing that the ops below\n        # have overloads to handle both float and Tensor lrs, so we just assert it's\n        # a float since most people using JIT are using floats\n        assert isinstance(lr, float)\n        assert isinstance(beta1, float)\n        assert isinstance(beta2, float)\n    else:\n        lr = _to_scalar(lr)\n        # TODO: Support nonzero-dim Tensor betas, see #147921\n\n    # We only shuffle around the beta when it is a Tensor, otherwise, we prefer\n    # treating it as a scalar.\n    # Note: ensure type declaration is under conditional check for isinstance\n    # or else torchscript will get cranky about the DeviceDict type.\n    if isinstance(beta1, Tensor):\n        beta1_dict: Optional[DeviceDtypeDict] = {(beta1.device, beta1.dtype): beta1}\n    else:\n        beta1_dict = None\n\n    for i, param in enumerate(params):\n        grad = grads[i] if not maximize else -grads[i]\n        exp_avg = exp_avgs[i]\n        exp_avg_sq = exp_avg_sqs[i]\n        step_t = state_steps[i]\n\n        # If compiling, the compiler will handle cudagraph checks, see note [torch.compile x capturable]\n        if not torch.compiler.is_compiling() and capturable:\n            capturable_supported_devices = _get_capturable_supported_devices()\n            assert (\n                param.device.type == step_t.device.type\n                and param.device.type in capturable_supported_devices\n            ), (\n                f\"If capturable=True, params and state_steps must be on supported devices: {capturable_supported_devices}.\"\n            )\n\n        # update step\n        step_t += 1\n\n        if weight_decay != 0:\n            if decoupled_weight_decay:\n                # Perform stepweight decay\n                param.mul_(1 - lr * weight_decay)\n            else:\n                # Nested if is necessary to bypass jitscript rules\n                if differentiable and isinstance(weight_decay, Tensor):\n                    if weight_decay.requires_grad:\n                        grad = grad.addcmul_(param.clone(), weight_decay)\n                    else:\n                        grad = grad.add(param, alpha=weight_decay)\n                else:\n                    grad = grad.add(param, alpha=weight_decay)\n\n        if torch.is_complex(param):\n            grad = torch.view_as_real(grad)\n            exp_avg = torch.view_as_real(exp_avg)\n            exp_avg_sq = torch.view_as_real(exp_avg_sq)\n            if amsgrad:\n                max_exp_avg_sqs[i] = torch.view_as_real(max_exp_avg_sqs[i])\n            param = torch.view_as_real(param)\n\n        device = param.device\n\n        if beta1_dict is not None:\n            dtype = param.dtype  # type: ignore[union-attr]\n\n            # cast to workaround https://github.com/pytorch/pytorch/issues/140601\n            key = (device, dtype)\n            if key not in beta1_dict:\n                beta1_dict[key] = beta1.to(  # type: ignore[union-attr]\n                    device=device, dtype=dtype, non_blocking=True\n                )\n\n            device_beta1: Union[float, Tensor] = beta1_dict[key]\n        else:\n            device_beta1 = beta1\n\n        # Decay the first and second moment running average coefficient\n        exp_avg.lerp_(grad, 1 - device_beta1)\n\n        # Nested if is necessary to bypass jitscript rules\n        if differentiable and isinstance(beta2, Tensor):\n            if beta2.requires_grad:\n                # Using lerp to only use 2 operations bc addcmul's value cannot be a tensor\n                # Showing equivalence of differentiable path and nondifferentiable path\n                # expavg * b2 + grad^2 * (1-b2)\n                #           add expavg * (1-b2) - expavg * (1-b2) = 0\n                # expavg * b2 + expavg * (1-b2) - expavg * (1-b2) + grad^2 * (1-b2)\n                # expavg - expavg * (1-b2) + grad^2 * (1-b2)\n                # expavg + (grad^2 - expavg) * (1-b2)\n                # expavg.lerp(grad^2, 1-beta2)\n                exp_avg_sq.lerp_(torch.square(grad), weight=1 - beta2)\n            else:\n                exp_avg_sq.mul_(beta2).addcmul_(\n                    grad, grad, value=cast(float, 1 - beta2)\n                )\n        else:\n            exp_avg_sq.mul_(beta2).addcmul_(grad, grad, value=1 - beta2)  # type: ignore[arg-type]\n\n        if capturable or differentiable:\n            step = step_t\n\n            # Nested if is necessary to bypass jitscript rules\n            if differentiable and isinstance(beta1, Tensor):\n                if beta1.requires_grad:\n                    bias_correction1 = 1 - beta1 ** step.clone()\n                else:\n                    bias_correction1 = 1 - beta1**step\n            else:\n                bias_correction1 = 1 - beta1**step\n\n            # Nested if is necessary to bypass jitscript rules\n            if differentiable and isinstance(beta2, Tensor):\n                if beta2.requires_grad:\n                    bias_correction2 = 1 - beta2 ** step.clone()\n                else:\n                    bias_correction2 = 1 - beta2**step\n            else:\n                bias_correction2 = 1 - beta2**step\n\n            step_size = lr / bias_correction1\n            step_size_neg = step_size.neg()\n\n            bias_correction2_sqrt = bias_correction2.sqrt()\n\n            if amsgrad:\n                # Maintains the maximum of all 2nd moment running avg. till now\n                if differentiable:\n                    max_exp_avg_sq = max_exp_avg_sqs[i].clone()\n                else:\n                    max_exp_avg_sq = max_exp_avg_sqs[i]\n\n                max_exp_avg_sqs[i].copy_(torch.maximum(max_exp_avg_sq, exp_avg_sq))\n\n                # Uses the max. for normalizing running avg. of gradient\n                # Folds in (admittedly ugly) 1-elem step_size math here to avoid extra param-set-sized read+write\n                # (can't fold it into addcdiv_ below because addcdiv_ requires value is a Number, not a Tensor)\n                denom = (\n                    max_exp_avg_sqs[i].sqrt() / (bias_correction2_sqrt * step_size_neg)\n                ).add_(eps / step_size_neg)\n            else:\n                denom = (\n                    exp_avg_sq.sqrt() / (bias_correction2_sqrt * step_size_neg)\n                ).add_(eps / step_size_neg)\n\n            if differentiable:\n                param.addcdiv_(exp_avg.clone(), denom)\n            else:\n                param.addcdiv_(exp_avg, denom)\n        else:\n            step = _get_value(step_t)\n\n            bias_correction1 = 1 - beta1**step\n            bias_correction2 = 1 - beta2**step\n\n            step_size = lr / bias_correction1\n\n            bias_correction2_sqrt = bias_correction2**0.5\n\n            if amsgrad:\n                # Maintains the maximum of all 2nd moment running avg. till now\n                torch.maximum(max_exp_avg_sqs[i], exp_avg_sq, out=max_exp_avg_sqs[i])\n\n                # Use the max. for normalizing running avg. of gradient\n                denom = (max_exp_avg_sqs[i].sqrt() / bias_correction2_sqrt).add_(eps)\n            else:\n                denom = (exp_avg_sq.sqrt() / bias_correction2_sqrt).add_(eps)\n\n            param.addcdiv_(exp_avg, denom, value=-step_size)  # wrapped it once now. The alpha is required to assure we go to the right overload.\n        if not torch.compiler.is_compiling() and device_state_steps[0].is_cpu:\n            torch._foreach_add_(\n                device_state_steps, torch.tensor(1.0, device=\"cpu\"), alpha=1.0\n            )\n        else:\n            torch._foreach_add_(device_state_steps, 1)\n\n        if weight_decay != 0:\n            if decoupled_weight_decay:\n                # we do not negate bias_correction1 as it'll need to be negated later anyway\n            torch._foreach_neg_(bias_correction2)\n\n            # foreach_div doesn't allow a scalar as the first arg\n            torch._foreach_div_(bias_correction1, lr)\n            torch._foreach_reciprocal_(bias_correction1)\n\n            torch._foreach_sqrt_(bias_correction2)\n\n            #  &\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                                 \\\\\n   206→            &\\textbf{input}      : \\alpha \\text{ (alpha)}, \\: \\gamma \\text{ (lr)},\n   207→ &\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                          \\\\[-1.ex]\n   233→       \\end{aligned}\n   234→\n   235→    For further details regarding the algorithm we refer to\n Hinton.\n   237→    and centered version `Generating Sequences\n   238→    With Recurrent Neural Networks <https://arxiv.org/pdf/1308.0850v5.pdf>`_.\n   239→    The implementation here takes the square root of the gradient average before\n   240→    adding epsilon (note that TensorFlow interchanges these two operations). The effective\n   241→    learning rate is thus :math:`\\gamma/(\\sqrt{v} + \\epsilon)` where :math:`\\gamma`\n   242→    is the scheduled learning rate and :math:`v` is the weighted moving average\n        )\n   404→\n   405→        # update step\n   406→        step_t += 1\n   407→\n   408→        if weight_decay != 0:\n   409→            if decoupled_weight_decay:\n   410→                # Perform stepweight decay\n   411→                param.mul_(1 - lr * weight_decay)\n   412→            else:\n   413→                # Nested if is necessary to bypass jitscript rules\n   414→                if differentiable and isinstance(weight_decay, Tensor):\n   415→                    if weight_decay.requires_grad:\n   416→                        grad = grad.addcmul_(param.clone(), weight_decay)\n   417→                    else:\n   418→                        grad = grad.add(param, alpha=weight_decay)\n   419→                else:\n   420→                    grad = grad.add(param, alpha=weight_decay)\n   421→\n   422→        if torch.is_complex(param):\n   423→            grad = torch.view_as_real(grad)\n   424→            exp_avg = torch.view_as_real(exp_avg)\n   425→            exp_avg_sq = torch.view_as_real(exp_avg_sq)\n   426→            if amsgrad:\n   427→                max_exp_avg_sqs[i] = torch.view_as_real(max_exp_avg_sqs[i])\n   428→            param = torch.view_as_real(param)\n   429→\n   430→        device = param.device\n   431→\n   432→        if beta1_dict is not None:\n   433→            dtype = param.dtype  # type: ignore[union-attr]\n   434→\n   435→            # cast to workaround https://github.com/pytorch/pytorch/issues/140601\n   436→            key = (device, dtype)\n   437→            if key not in beta1_dict:\n   438→                beta1_dict[key] = beta1.to(  # type: ignore[union-attr]\n   439→                    device=device, dtype=dtype, non_blocking=True\n   440→                )\n   441→\n   442→            device_beta1: Union[float, Tensor] = beta1_dict[key]\n   443→        else:\n   444→            device_beta1 = beta1\n   445→\n   446→        # Decay the first and second moment running average coefficient\n   447→        exp_avg.lerp_(grad, 1 - device_beta1)\n   448→\n   449→        # Nested if is necessary to bypass jitscript rules\n   450→        if differentiable and isinstance(beta2, Tensor):\n   451→            if beta2.requires_grad:\n   452→                # Using lerp to only use 2 operations bc addcmul's value cannot be a tensor\n   453→                # Showing equivalence of differentiable path and nondifferentiable path\n   454→                # expavg * b2 + grad^2 * (1-b2)\n   455→                #           add expavg * (1-b2) - expavg * (1-b2) = 0\n   456→                # expavg * b2 + expavg * (1-b2) - expavg * (1-b2) + grad^2 * (1-b2)\n   457→                # expavg - expavg * (1-b2) + grad^2 * (1-b2)\n   458→                # expavg + (grad^2 - expavg) * (1-b2)\n   459→                # expavg.lerp(grad^2, 1-beta2)\n   460→                exp_avg_sq.lerp_(torch.square(grad), weight=1 - beta2)\n   461→            else:\n   462→                exp_avg_sq.mul_(beta2).addcmul_(\n   463→                    grad, grad, value=cast(float, 1 - beta2)\n   464→                )\n   465→        else:\n   466→            exp_avg_sq.mul_(beta2).addcmul_(grad, grad, value=1 - beta2)  # type: ignore[arg-type]\n   467→\n   468→        if capturable or differentiable:\n   469→            step = step_t\n   470→\n   471→            # Nested if is necessary to bypass jitscript rules\n   472→            if differentiable and isinstance(beta1, Tensor):\n   473→                if beta1.requires_grad:\n   474→                    bias_correction1 = 1 - beta1 ** step.clone()\n   475→                else:\n   476→                    bias_correction1 = 1 - beta1**step\n   477→            else:\n   478→                bias_correction1 = 1 - beta1**step\n   479→\n   480→            # Nested if is necessary to bypass jitscript rules\n   481→            if differentiable and isinstance(beta2, Tensor):\n   482→                if beta2.requires_grad:\n   483→                    bias_correction2 = 1 - beta2 ** step.clone()\n   484→                else:\n   485→                    bias_correction2 = 1 - beta2**step\n   486→            else:\n   487→                bias_correction2 = 1 - beta2**step\n   488→\n   489→            step_size = lr / bias_correction1\n   490→            step_size_neg = step_size.neg()\n   491→\n   492→            bias_correction2_sqrt = bias_correction2.sqrt()\n   493→\n   494→            if amsgrad:\n   495→                # Maintains the maximum of all 2nd moment running avg. till now\n   496→                if differentiable:\n   497→                    max_exp_avg_sq = max_exp_avg_sqs[i].clone()\n   498→                else:\n   499→                    max_exp_avg_sq = max_exp_avg_sqs[i]\n   500→\n   501→                max_exp_avg_sqs[i].copy_(torch.maximum(max_exp_avg_sq, exp_avg_sq))\n   502→\n   503→                # Uses the max. for normalizing running avg. of gradient\n   504→                # Folds in (admittedly ugly) 1-elem step_size math here to avoid extra param-set-sized read+write\n   505→                # (can't fold it into addcdiv_ below because addcdiv_ requires value is a Number, not a Tensor)\n   506→                denom = (\n   507→                    max_exp_avg_sqs[i].sqrt() / (bias_correction2_sqrt * step_size_neg)\n   508→                ).add_(eps / step_size_neg)\n   509→            else:\n   510→                denom = (\n   511→                    exp_avg_sq.sqrt() / (bias_correction2_sqrt * step_size_neg)\n   512→                ).add_(eps / step_size_neg)\n   513→\n   514→            if differentiable:\n   515→                param.addcdiv_(exp_avg.clone(), denom)\n   516→            else:\n   517→                param.addcdiv_(exp_avg, denom)\n   518→        else:\n   519→            step = _get_value(step_t)\n   520→\n   521→            bias_correction1 = 1 - beta1**step\n   522→            bias_correction2 = 1 - beta2**step\n   523→\n   524→            step_size = lr / bias_correction1\n   525→\n   526→            bias_correction2_sqrt = bias_correction2**0.5\n   527→\n   528→            if amsgrad:\n   529→                # Maintains the maximum of all 2nd moment running avg. till now\n   530→                torch.maximum(max_exp_avg_sqs[i], exp_avg_sq, out=max_exp_avg_sqs[i])\n   531→\n   532→                # Use the max. for normalizing running avg. of gradient\n   533→                denom = (max_exp_avg_sqs[i].sqrt() / bias_correction2_sqrt).add_(eps)\n   534→            else:\n   535→                denom = (exp_avg_sq.sqrt() / bias_correction2_sqrt).add_(eps)\n   536→\n   537→            param.addcdiv_(exp_avg, denom, value=-step_size)  # type: ignore[arg-type]\n   538→\n   539→        # Lastly, switch back to complex view\n   540→        if amsgrad and torch.is_complex(params[i]):\n   541→            max_exp_avg_sqs[i] = torch.view_as_complex(max_exp_avg_sqs[i])\n   542→\n   543→\n   544→def _multi_tensor_adam(\n   545→    params: list[Tensor],\n   546→    grads: list[Tensor],\n   547→    exp_avgs: list[Tensor],\n   548→    exp_avg_sqs: list[Tensor],\n   549→    max_exp_avg_sqs: list[Tensor],\n   550→    state_steps: list[Tensor],\n   551→    grad_scale: Optional[Tensor],\n   552→    found_inf: Optional[Tensor],\n   553→    *,\n   554→    amsgrad: bool,\n   555→    has_complex: bool,\n   556→    beta1: Union[float, Tensor],\n   557→    beta2: Union[float, Tensor],\n   558→    lr: Union[float, Tensor],\n   559→    weight_decay: float,\n   560→    eps: float,\n   561→    maximize: bool,\n   562→    capturable: bool,\n   563→    differentiable: bool,\n   564→    decoupled_weight_decay: bool,\n   565→):\n   566→    if len(params) == 0:\n   567→        return\n   568→\n   569→    if isinstance(lr, Tensor):\n   570→        if not capturable:\n   571→            raise RuntimeError(\n   572→                \"lr as a Tensor is not supported for capturable=False and foreach=True\"\n   573→            )\n   574→        if lr.numel() != 1:\n   575→            raise ValueError(\"Tensor lr must be 1-element\")\n   576→\n   577→    if isinstance(beta1, Tensor):\n   578→        if not capturable:\n   579→            raise ValueError(\n   580→                \"beta1 as a Tensor is not supported for capturable=False and foreach=True\"\n   581→            )\n   582→        if beta1.numel() != 1:\n   583→            raise ValueError(\"Tensor beta1 must be 1-element\")\n   584→\n   585→    if isinstance(beta2, Tensor):\n   586→        if not capturable:\n   587→            raise ValueError(\n   588→                \"beta2 as a Tensor is not supported for capturable=False and foreach=True\"\n   589→            )\n   590→        if beta2.numel() != 1:\n   591→            raise ValueError(\"Tensor beta2 must be 1-element\")\n   592→\n   593→    # If compiling, the compiler will handle cudagraph checks, see note [torch.compile x capturable]\n   594→    if not torch.compiler.is_compiling() and capturable:\n   595→        capturable_supported_devices = _get_capturable_supported_devices(\n   596→            supports_xla=False\n   597→        )\n   598→        assert all(\n   599→            p.device.type == step.device.type\n   600→            and p.device.type in capturable_supported_devices\n   601→            for p, step in zip(params, state_steps)\n   602→        ), (\n   603→            f\"If capturable=True, params and state_steps must be on supported devices: {capturable_supported_devices}.\"\n   604→        )\n   605→\n   606→    assert grad_scale is None and found_inf is None\n   607→\n   608→    assert not differentiable, \"_foreach ops don't support autograd\"\n   609→\n   610→    lr = _to_scalar(lr)\n   611→    # TODO: Support nonzero-dim Tensor betas, see #147921\n   612→\n   613→    grouped_tensors = Optimizer._group_tensors_by_device_and_dtype(\n   614→        [params, grads, exp_avgs, exp_avg_sqs, max_exp_avg_sqs, state_steps]  # type: ignore[list-item]\n   615→    )\n   616→\n   617→    # We only shuffle around the beta when it is a Tensor and on CUDA, otherwise, we prefer\n   618→    # treating it as a scalar.\n   619→    beta1_dict: Optional[DeviceDict] = (  # type: ignore[attr-defined]\n   620→        {beta1.device: beta1}\n   621→        if isinstance(beta1, Tensor) and str(beta1.device) != \"cpu\"\n   622→        else None\n   623→    )\n   624→\n   625→    for (\n   626→        device_params_,\n   627→        device_grads_,\n   628→        device_exp_avgs_,\n   629→        device_exp_avg_sqs_,\n   630→        device_max_exp_avg_sqs_,\n   631→        device_state_steps_,\n   632→    ), _ in grouped_tensors.values():\n   633→        device_params = cast(list[Tensor], device_params_)\n   634→        device_grads = cast(list[Tensor], device_grads_)\n   635→        device_exp_avgs = cast(list[Tensor], device_exp_avgs_)\n   636→        device_exp_avg_sqs = cast(list[Tensor], device_exp_avg_sqs_)\n   637→        device_state_steps = cast(list[Tensor], device_state_steps_)\n   638→\n   639→        device = device_params[0].device\n   640→        if beta1_dict is not None and device not in beta1_dict:\n   641→            beta1_dict[device] = beta1.to(device=device, non_blocking=True)  # type: ignore[union-attr, attr-defined]\n   642→\n   643→        device_beta1 = beta1_dict[device] if beta1_dict else beta1\n   644→\n   645→        # Handle complex parameters\n   646→        if has_complex:\n   647→            if amsgrad:\n   648→                device_max_exp_avg_sqs = cast(list[Tensor], device_max_exp_avg_sqs_)\n   649→                _view_as_real(\n   650→                    device_params,\n   651→                    device_grads,\n   652→                    device_exp_avgs,\n   653→                    device_exp_avg_sqs,\n   654→                    device_max_exp_avg_sqs,\n   655→                )\n   656→            else:\n   657→                _view_as_real(\n   658→                    device_params, device_grads, device_exp_avgs, device_exp_avg_sqs\n   659→                )\n   660→\n   661→        if maximize:\n   662→            device_grads = torch._foreach_neg(device_grads)  # type: ignore[assignment]\n   663→\n   664→        # Update steps\n   665→        # If steps are on CPU, foreach will fall back to the slow path, which is a for-loop calling t.add(1) over\n   666→        # and over. 1 will then be wrapped into a Tensor over and over again, which is slower than if we just\n   667→        # wrapped it once now. The alpha is required to assure we go to the right overload.\n   668→        if not torch.compiler.is_compiling() and device_state_steps[0].is_cpu:\n   669→            torch._foreach_add_(\n   670→                device_state_steps, torch.tensor(1.0, device=\"cpu\"), alpha=1.0\n   671→            )\n   672→        else:\n   673→            torch._foreach_add_(device_state_steps, 1)\n   674→\n   675→        if weight_decay != 0:\n   676→            if decoupled_weight_decay:\n   677→                # Perform stepweight decay\n   678→                torch._foreach_mul_(device_params, 1 - lr * weight_decay)\n   679→            else:\n   680→                # Reuse the intermediate memory (device_grads) already allocated for maximize\n   681→                if maximize:\n   682→                    torch._foreach_add_(device_grads, device_params, alpha=weight_decay)\n   683→                else:\n   684→                    device_grads = torch._foreach_add(  # type: ignore[assignment]\n   685→                        device_grads, device_params, alpha=weight_decay\n   686→                    )\n   687→\n   688→        # Decay the first and second moment running average coefficient\n   689→        # Use device beta1 if beta1 is a tensor to ensure all\n   690→        # tensors are on the same device\n   691→        torch._foreach_lerp_(\n   692→            device_exp_avgs, device_grads, cast(float, 1 - device_beta1)\n   693→        )\n   694→\n   695→        torch._foreach_mul_(device_exp_avg_sqs, beta2)\n   696→\n   697→        # Due to the strictness of the _foreach_addcmul API, we can't have a single\n   698→        # tensor scalar as the scalar arg (only python number is supported there)\n   699→        # as a result, separate out the value mul\n   700→        # Filed https://github.com/pytorch/pytorch/issues/139795\n   701→        if isinstance(beta2, torch.Tensor):\n   702→            scaled_device_grads = torch._foreach_mul(device_grads, 1 - beta2)  # type: ignore[assignment]\n   703→            value = 1.0\n   704→        else:\n   705→            scaled_device_grads = device_grads  # type: ignore[assignment]\n   706→            value = 1 - beta2\n   707→\n   708→        torch._foreach_addcmul_(\n   709→            device_exp_avg_sqs, scaled_device_grads, device_grads, value\n   710→        )\n   711→\n   712→        # Delete the local intermediate(s) since they won't be used anymore to save on peak memory\n   713→        del device_grads\n   714→        del scaled_device_grads\n   715→\n   716→        bias_correction1: Union[tuple[Tensor, ...], list[Tensor]]\n   717→        bias_correction2: Union[tuple[Tensor, ...], list[Tensor]]\n   718→        bias_correction2_sqrt: Union[tuple[Tensor, ...], list[Tensor]]\n   719→\n   720→        if capturable:\n   721→            bias_correction1 = torch._foreach_pow(beta1, device_state_steps)  # type: ignore[arg-type]\n   722→            bias_correction2 = torch._foreach_pow(beta2, device_state_steps)  # type: ignore[arg-type]\n   723→            # foreach_sub doesn't allow a scalar as the first arg\n   724→            torch._foreach_sub_(bias_correction1, 1)\n   725→            torch._foreach_sub_(bias_correction2, 1)\n   726→            # we do not negate bias_correction1 as it'll need to be negated later anyway\n   727→            torch._foreach_neg_(bias_correction2)\n   728→\n   729→            # foreach_div doesn't allow a scalar as the first arg\n   730→            torch._foreach_div_(bias_correction1, lr)\n   731→            torch._foreach_reciprocal_(bias_correction1)\n   732→\n   733→            torch._foreach_sqrt_(bias_correction2)\n   734→\n   735→            # Re-assign for clarity as we maintain minimal intermediates: we'll have\n   736→            # step_size = - lr / (1 - beta1 ^ t) where t = num_steps\n   737→            # bias_correction2_sqrt = sqrt(1 - beta2 ^ t)\n   738→            step_size = bias_correction1\n   739→            bias_correction2_sqrt = bias_correction2\n   740→\n   741→            if amsgrad:\n   742→                device_max_exp_avg_sqs = cast(list[Tensor], device_max_exp_avg_sqs_)\n   743→                # Maintains the maximum of all 2nd moment running avg. till now\n   744→                torch._foreach_maximum_(device_max_exp_avg_sqs, device_exp_avg_sqs)  # type: ignore[assignment]\n   745→\n   746→                # Set intermediate to the max. for normalizing running avg. of gradient when amsgrad\n   747→                exp_avg_sq_sqrt = torch._foreach_sqrt(device_max_exp_avg_sqs)\n   748→            else:\n   749→                exp_avg_sq_sqrt = torch._foreach_sqrt(device_exp_avg_sqs)\n   750→\n   751→            torch._foreach_div_(exp_avg_sq_sqrt, bias_correction2_sqrt)\n   752→            torch._foreach_add_(exp_avg_sq_sqrt, eps)\n   753→            torch._foreach_div_(exp_avg_sq_sqrt, step_size)\n   754→\n   755→            # at this point, exp_avg_sq_sqrt = - (1 - beta^t) * [sqrt(exp_avg_sq / (1 - beta2^t)) + eps] / lr\n   756→            torch._foreach_addcdiv_(device_params, device_exp_avgs, exp_avg_sq_sqrt)\n   757→        else:\n   758→            bias_correction1 = [\n   759→                1 - beta1 ** _get_value(step) for step in device_state_steps\n   760→            ]\n   761→            bias_correction2 = [\n   762→                1 - beta2 ** _get_value(step) for step in device_state_steps\n   763→            ]\n   764→\n   765→            step_size = _stack_if_compiling([(lr / bc) * -1 for bc in bias_correction1])\n   766→\n   767→            bias_correction2_sqrt = [bc**0.5 for bc in bias_correction2]  # type: ignore[arg-type]\n   768→\n   769→            if amsgrad:\n   770→                device_max_exp_avg_sqs = cast(list[Tensor], device_max_exp_avg_sqs_)\n   771→                # Maintains the maximum of all 2nd moment running avg. till now\n   772→                torch._foreach_maximum_(device_max_exp_avg_sqs, device_exp_avg_sqs)\n   773→\n   774→                # Use the max. for normalizing running avg. of gradient\n   775→                exp_avg_sq_sqrt = torch._foreach_sqrt(device_max_exp_avg_sqs)\n   776→            else:\n   777→                exp_avg_sq_sqrt = torch._foreach_sqrt(device_exp_avg_sqs)\n   778→\n   779→            torch._foreach_div_(exp_avg_sq_sqrt, bias_correction2_sqrt)\n   780→            torch._foreach_add_(exp_avg_sq_sqrt, eps)\n   781→            torch._foreach_addcdiv_(\n   782→                device_params,\n   783→                device_exp_avgs,\n   784→                exp_avg_sq_sqrt,\n   785→                step_size,  # type: ignore[arg-type]\n   786→            )\n   787→\n   788→\n   789→def _fused_adam(\n   790→    params: list[Tensor],\n   791→    grads: list[Tensor],\n   792→    exp_avgs: list[Tensor],\n   793→    exp_avg_sqs: list[Tensor],\n   794→    max_exp_avg_sqs: list[Tensor],\n   795→    state_steps: list[Tensor],\n   796→    grad_scale: Optional[Tensor],\n   797→    found_inf: Optional[Tensor],\n   798→    *,\n   799→    amsgrad: bool,\n   800→    has_complex: bool,  # Needed for consistency.\n   801→    beta1: float,\n   802→    beta2: float,\n   803→    lr: Union[float, Tensor],\n   804→    weight_decay: float,\n   805→    eps: float,\n   806→    maximize: bool,\n   807→    capturable: bool,  # Needed for consistency.\n   808→    differentiable: bool,\n   809→    decoupled_weight_decay: bool,\n   810→) -> None:\n   811→    if not params:\n   812→        return\n   813→    if differentiable:\n   814→        raise RuntimeError(\"Adam with fused=True does not support differentiable=True\")\n   815→\n   816→    grad_scale_dict: DeviceDict = (\n   817→        {grad_scale.device: grad_scale} if grad_scale is not None else {}\n   818→    )\n   819→    found_inf_dict: DeviceDict = (\n   820→        {found_inf.device: found_inf} if found_inf is not None else {}\n   821→    )\n   822→\n   823→    # We only shuffle around the lr when it is a Tensor and on CUDA, otherwise, we prefer\n   824→    # treating it as a scalar.\n   825→    lr_dict: Optional[DeviceDict] = (\n   826→        {lr.device: lr} if isinstance(lr, Tensor) and str(lr.device) != \"cpu\" else None\n   827→    )\n   828→    grouped_tensors = Optimizer._group_tensors_by_device_and_dtype(\n   829→        [params, grads, exp_avgs, exp_avg_sqs, max_exp_avg_sqs, state_steps]  # type: ignore[list-item]\n   830→    )\n   831→    for (device, _), (\n   832→        (\n   833→            device_params_,\n   834→            device_grads_,\n   835→            device_exp_avgs_,\n   836→            device_exp_avg_sqs_,\n   837→            device_max_exp_avg_sqs,\n   838→            device_state_steps_,\n   839→        ),\n   840→        _,\n   841→    ) in grouped_tensors.items():\n   842→        device_params = cast(list[Tensor], device_params_)\n   843→        device_grads = cast(list[Tensor], device_grads_)\n   844→        device_exp_avgs = cast(list[Tensor], device_exp_avgs_)\n   845→        device_exp_avg_sqs = cast(list[Tensor], device_exp_avg_sqs_)\n   846→        device_state_steps = cast(list[Tensor], device_state_steps_)\n   847→\n   848→        device_grad_scale, device_found_inf = None, None\n   849→        if grad_scale is not None:\n   850→            device_grad_scale = grad_scale_dict.setdefault(\n   851→                device, grad_scale.to(device, non_blocking=True)\n   852→            )\n   853→        if found_inf is not None:\n   854→            device_found_inf = found_inf_dict.setdefault(\n   855→                device, found_inf.to(device, non_blocking=True)\n   856→            )\n   857→        if lr_dict is not None and device not in lr_dict:\n   858→            lr_dict[device] = lr.to(device=device, non_blocking=True)  # `torch._foreach_sub_()` - subtraction\n- `torch._foreach_div_()` - division\n- `torch._foreach_sqrt_()` - square root\n- `torch._foreach_neg_()` - negation\n- `torch._foreach_reciprocal_()` - 1/x\n- `torch._foreach_abs_()` - absolute value\n- `torch._foreach_pow()` - exponentiation\n- `torch._foreach_maximum_()` - element-wise max\n\n**Binary operations (in-place):**\n- `torch._foreach_addcmul_()` - fused multiply-add: y += x1 * x2 * value\n- `torch._foreach_addcdiv_()` - fused divide-add: y += x1 / x2 * value\n- `torch._foreach_lerp_()` - linear interpolation\n\n**Copy/allocation:**\n- `torch._foreach_add()` - returns new tensor (not in-place)\n- `torch._foreach_mul()` - returns new tensor\n- `torch._foreach_sub()` - returns new tensor\n- `torch._foreach_sqrt()` - returns new tensor\n- `torch._foreach_abs()` - returns new tensor\n- `torch._foreach_maximum()` - returns new tensor\n\n### 8. **Memory Efficiency Patterns**\n\n#### A. in-place\n    # grads now contains: -grad + weight_decay * param\n    # This buffer is reused for next operations\nelse:\n    device_grads = torch._foreach_add(device_grads, device_params, alpha=weight_decay)\n    # Creates new tensor, original grads not modified\n```\n\n#### B. **Temporary Buffer Deletion**\n```python\n# Explicitly delete large intermediates to free memory\ndel device_grads\ndel scaled_device_grads\n```\n- Appears in: Adam\n\n### 9. **Type Checking and Conversion Patterns**\n\n**Type casting:**\n```python\nfrom typing import cast, Optional, These 11+ optimizer files currently duplicate substantial amounts of common infrastructure code, making maintenance difficult and preventing consistent improvements.\n\nThe goal is to extract repeated patterns into a shared `torch/optim/_foreach.py` module while maintaining 100% backward compatibility with public APIs.\n\n## Problem Statement\n**Current state:** 11 optimizer files each contain a `_multi_tensor_*` function with 200-400+ lines of code\n- Step counter updates (CPU optimization) - duplicated 8+ times\n- Weight decay + maximize pattern - duplicated 7+ times\n- Complex number conversion - duplicated 7+ times\n- Device/dtype grouping + casting - duplicated in every file\n- Sparse gradient checks - several files\n\nThis duplication makes it difficult to:\n- Fix bugs consistently across all optimizers\n- Add features (e.g., AMP support) to all optimizers uniformly\n- Understand the core algorithm vs infrastructure code\n\n## Solution Overview\nCreate a new `torch/optim/_foreach.py` module with reusable helper functions extracted from the common patterns identified across all `_multi_tensor_*` implementations.\n\n### Key Design Principles\n1. **Don't over-engineer**: Only extract code that is actually duplicated across 2+ optimizers\n2. **Keep algorithm-specific logic in optimizer files**: Each optimizer's core algorithm stays in its file\n3. **Focus on infrastructure**: Extract device/dtype grouping, step updates, complex handling, maximize, weight decay utilities\n4. **Backward compatibility**: All public APIs remain unchanged; this is purely internal refactoring\n5. **Minimal dependencies**: New module should depend only on torch and optimizer.py utilities\n\n## Implementation Plan\n\n### Phase 1: Create `torch/optim/_foreach.py` Module\nCreate new file with shared helper functions based on duplicated patterns:\n\n**File: `/workspace/torch/optim/_foreach.py`**\n\nFunctions to extract (in priority order of duplication):\n\n1. **`_apply_weight_decay_and_maximize(grads, params, weight_decay, maximize)`**\n   - Combines the maximize negation + weight decay application pattern\n   - Handles memory reuse when both operations are needed\n   - Used in: SGD, Adam, Adagrad, Adamax, Adadelta, ASGD, RMSprop (7+ files)\n\n2. **`_update_step_counters(state_steps, is_compiling)`**\n   - Applies the CPU-specific step update optimization\n   - Avoids repeated torch.tensor() allocations\n   - Used in: Adam, Adamax, Adadelta, ASGD, RMSprop, Rprop, NAdam, RAdam (8+ files)\n\n3. **`_apply_complex_view_if_needed(has_complex, params, grads, *state_tensors)`**\n   - Converts complex tensors to real view for processing\n   - Used in: Adam, Adagrad, Adamax, Adadelta, ASGD, RMSprop, Rprop, NAdam (7+ files)\n\n4. **`_handle_capturable_bias_correction(betas, state_steps, lr, capturable, is_compiling)`**\n   - Unified capturable vs non-capturable bias correction logic\n   - Returns appropriate tensor or list of scalars\n   - Used in: Adam, Adamax, Adadelta, ASGD, RMSprop, Rprop, NAdam\n\n5. **`_validate_foreach_inputs(params, grad_scale, found_inf, differentiable, function_name)`**\n   - Centralize validation logic for foreach operations\n   - Check empty params, AMP assertions, etc.\n\n### Phase 2: Update Optimizer Files (Priority Order)\nUpdate the following files to import and use helpers from `_foreach.py`:\n\n1. **`torch/optim/sgd.py`** (_multi_tensor_sgd)\n   - Replace weight_decay + maximize logic with shared function\n   - Straightforward refactoring - minimal algorithm complexity\n\n2. **`torch/optim/adam.py`** (_multi_tensor_adam)\n   - Replace weight_decay + maximize logic\n   - Replace step update logic\n   - Replace complex number handling\n   - Keep bias correction logic (may share later)\n\n3. **`torch/optim/adamax.py`** (_multi_tensor_adamax)\n   - Same pattern as Adam\n\n4. **`torch/optim/rmsprop.py`** (_multi_tensor_rmsprop)\n   - Replace step update logic\n   - Replace complex number handling\n   - Replace weight_decay + maximize logic\n\n5. **`torch/optim/adadelta.py`** (_multi_tensor_adadelta)\n   - Similar to RMSprop pattern\n\n6. **`torch/optim/adagrad.py`** (_multi_tensor_adagrad)\n   - Has sparse handling - needs careful refactoring\n\n7. Others as time permits (ASGD, NAdam, RAdam, Rprop, Radadelta if needed)\n\n### Phase 3: Testing Strategy\n1. **Compile test** - Ensure no import/syntax errors\n2. **Run existing optimizer tests** - All should pass unchanged\n   - `python -m pytest test/test_optim.py -v` (or equivalent)\n3. **Numerical equivalence** - Foreach results vs single-tensor should match\n4. **Edge cases** - Empty params, single param, multi-device, etc.\n\n## Critical Implementation Details\n\n### Signature Patterns (Do NOT break)\nAll functions must maintain existing signatures - no changes to public optimizer APIs:\n- `sgd(params, d_p_list, momentum_buffer_list, ..., foreach=None, ...)`\n- `adam(params, grads, exp_avgs, ..., foreach=None, ...)`\n- All dispatch logic stays in optimizer files\n\n### What Stays in Optimizer Files\n- Dispatcher functions (sgd, adam, etc.) that choose single_tensor vs multi_tensor vs fused\n- Optimizer class definitions and state management\n- Algorithm-specific logic that's unique to each optimizer\n- Public docstrings and examples\n\n### What Moves to `_foreach.py`\n- Utility functions for common operations\n- Grouping/casting infrastructure\n- Step counter updates\n- Maximize + weight decay utilities\n- Complex number handling helpers\n- Validation helpers\n\n## Files to Modify\n1. **Create:** `/workspace/torch/optim/_foreach.py` (NEW)\n2. **Update:** `/workspace/torch/optim/sgd.py`\n3. **Update:** `/workspace/torch/optim/adam.py`\n4. **Update:** `/workspace/torch/optim/adamax.py`\n5. **Update:** `/workspace/torch/optim/rmsprop.py`\n6. **Update:** `/workspace/torch/optim/adadelta.py`\n7. **Update:** `/workspace/torch/optim/adagrad.py`\n8. *Others as time permits*\n\n## Success Criteria\n- [ ] `_foreach.py` module created with helper functions\n- [ ] At least 3 optimizer files (SGD, Adam, RMSprop) updated to use shared helpers\n- [ ] All existing tests pass without modification\n- [ ] Numerical equivalence verified (single-tensor vs multi-tensor outputs match)\n- [ ] Code duplication reduced by 30%+ across updated files\n- [ ] No changes to public APIs or behavior\n\n## Implementation Order\n1. Create `_foreach.py` with most duplicated helpers (weight decay + maximize)\n2. Update SGD first (simplest, good validation)\n3. Update Adam (most complex, highest impact)\n4. Update RMSprop (validates different algorithm type)\n5. Update remaining files if time permits\n\n## Validation Approach\nAfter each optimizer update:\n- Run tests for that optimizer specifically\n- Verify numerical equivalence with single-tensor implementation\n- Check import paths work correctly\n- Ensure backward compatibility\n\n## Rollback Strategy\nIf any optimizer breaks:\n- Revert that specific optimizer file to original\n- Investigate root cause in shared helper\n- Fix helper function\n- Re-attempt update\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":9,"cache_creation_input_tokens":4100,"cache_read_input_tokens":54800,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":4100},"output_tokens":4,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"3e0addbe-3a14-4b81-856f-09cdbc90aa87","uuid":"c94b8f6d-ea4d-45ef-91d9-98f7aabfc761"}

These 11+ optimizer files currently duplicate substantial amounts of common infrastructure code, making maintenance difficult and preventing consistent improvements.\n\nThe goal is to extract repeated patterns into a shared `torch/optim/_foreach.py` module while maintaining 100% backward compatibility with public APIs.\n\n## Problem Statement\n**Current state:** 11 optimizer files each contain a `_multi_tensor_*` function with 200-400+ lines of code\n- Step counter updates (CPU optimization) - duplicated 8+ times\n- Weight decay + maximize pattern - duplicated 7+ times\n- Complex number conversion - duplicated 7+ times\n- Device/dtype grouping + casting - duplicated in every file\n- Sparse gradient checks - several files\n\nThis duplication makes it difficult to:\n- Fix bugs consistently across all optimizers\n- Add features (e.g., AMP support) to all optimizers uniformly\n- Understand the core algorithm vs infrastructure code\n\n## Solution Overview\nCreate a new `torch/optim/_foreach.py` module with reusable helper functions extracted from the common patterns identified across all `_multi_tensor_*` implementations.\n\n### Key Design Principles\n1. **Don't over-engineer**: Only extract code that is actually duplicated across 2+ optimizers\n2. **Keep algorithm-specific logic in optimizer files**: Each optimizer's core algorithm stays in its file\n3. **Focus on infrastructure**: Extract device/dtype grouping, step updates, complex handling, maximize, weight decay utilities\n4. **Backward compatibility**: All public APIs remain unchanged; this is purely internal refactoring\n5. **Minimal dependencies**: New module should depend only on torch and optimizer.py utilities\n\n## Implementation Plan\n\n### Phase 1: Create `torch/optim/_foreach.py` Module\nCreate new file with shared helper functions based on duplicated patterns:\n\n**File: `/workspace/torch/optim/_foreach.py`**\n\nFunctions to extract (in priority order of duplication):\n\n1. **`_apply_weight_decay_and_maximize(grads, params, weight_decay, maximize)`**\n   - Combines the maximize negation + weight decay application pattern\n   - Handles memory reuse when both operations are needed\n   - Used in: SGD, Adam, Adagrad, Adamax, Adadelta, ASGD, RMSprop (7+ files)\n\n2. **`_update_step_counters(state_steps, is_compiling)`**\n   - Applies the CPU-specific step update optimization\n   - Avoids repeated torch.tensor() allocations\n   - Used in: Adam, Adamax, Adadelta, ASGD, RMSprop, Rprop, NAdam, RAdam (8+ files)\n\n3. **`_apply_complex_view_if_needed(has_complex, params, grads, *state_tensors)`**\n   - Converts complex tensors to real view for processing\n   - Used in: Adam, Adagrad, Adamax, Adadelta, ASGD, RMSprop, Rprop, NAdam (7+ files)\n\n4. **`_handle_capturable_bias_correction(betas, state_steps, lr, capturable, is_compiling)`**\n   - Unified capturable vs non-capturable bias correction logic\n   - Returns appropriate tensor or list of scalars\n   - Used in: Adam, Adamax, Adadelta, ASGD, RMSprop, Rprop, NAdam\n\n5. **`_validate_foreach_inputs(params, grad_scale, found_inf, differentiable, function_name)`**\n   - Centralize validation logic for foreach operations\n   - Check empty params, AMP assertions, etc.\n\n### Phase 2: Update Optimizer Files (Priority Order)\nUpdate the following files to import and use helpers from `_foreach.py`:\n\n1. **`torch/optim/sgd.py`** (_multi_tensor_sgd)\n   - Replace weight_decay + maximize logic with shared function\n   - Straightforward refactoring - minimal algorithm complexity\n\n2. **`torch/optim/adam.py`** (_multi_tensor_adam)\n   - Replace weight_decay + maximize logic\n   - Replace step update logic\n   - Replace complex number handling\n   - Keep bias correction logic (may share later)\n\n3. **`torch/optim/adamax.py`** (_multi_tensor_adamax)\n   - Same pattern as Adam\n\n4. **`torch/optim/rmsprop.py`** (_multi_tensor_rmsprop)\n   - Replace step update logic\n   - Replace complex number handling\n   - Replace weight_decay + maximize logic\n\n5. **`torch/optim/adadelta.py`** (_multi_tensor_adadelta)\n   - Similar to RMSprop pattern\n\n6. **`torch/optim/adagrad.py`** (_multi_tensor_adagrad)\n   - Has sparse handling - needs careful refactoring\n\n7. Others as time permits (ASGD, NAdam, RAdam, Rprop, Radadelta if needed)\n\n### Phase 3: Testing Strategy\n1. **Compile test** - Ensure no import/syntax errors\n2. **Run existing optimizer tests** - All should pass unchanged\n   - `python -m pytest test/test_optim.py -v` (or equivalent)\n3. **Numerical equivalence** - Foreach results vs single-tensor should match\n4. **Edge cases** - Empty params, single param, multi-device, etc.\n\n## Critical Implementation Details\n\n### Signature Patterns (Do NOT break)\nAll functions must maintain existing signatures - no changes to public optimizer APIs:\n- `sgd(params, d_p_list, momentum_buffer_list, ..., foreach=None, ...)`\n- `adam(params, grads, exp_avgs, ..., foreach=None, ...)`\n- All dispatch logic stays in optimizer files\n\n### What Stays in Optimizer Files\n- Dispatcher functions (sgd, adam, etc.) that choose single_tensor vs multi_tensor vs fused\n- Optimizer class definitions and state management\n- Algorithm-specific logic that's unique to each optimizer\n- Public docstrings and examples\n\n### What Moves to `_foreach.py`\n- Utility functions for common operations\n- Grouping/casting infrastructure\n- Step counter updates\n- Maximize + weight decay utilities\n- Complex number handling helpers\n- Validation helpers\n\n## Files to Modify\n1. **Create:** `/workspace/torch/optim/_foreach.py` (NEW)\n2. **Update:** `/workspace/torch/optim/sgd.py`\n3. **Update:** `/workspace/torch/optim/adam.py`\n4. **Update:** `/workspace/torch/optim/adamax.py`\n5. **Update:** `/workspace/torch/optim/rmsprop.py`\n6. **Update:** `/workspace/torch/optim/adadelta.py`\n7. **Update:** `/workspace/torch/optim/adagrad.py`\n8. *Others as time permits*\n\n## Success Criteria\n- [ ] `_foreach.py` module created with helper functions\n- [ ] At least 3 optimizer files (SGD, Adam, RMSprop) updated to use shared helpers\n- [ ] All existing tests pass without modification\n- [ ] Numerical equivalence verified (single-tensor vs multi-tensor outputs match)\n- [ ] Code duplication reduced by 30%+ across updated files\n- [ ] No changes to public APIs or behavior\n\n## Implementation Order\n1. Create `_foreach.py` with most duplicated helpers (weight decay + maximize)\n2. Update SGD first (simplest, good validation)\n3. Update Adam (most complex, highest impact)\n4. Update RMSprop (validates different algorithm type)\n5. Update remaining files if time permits\n\n## Validation Approach\nAfter each optimizer update:\n- Run tests for that optimizer specifically\n- Verify numerical equivalence with single-tensor implementation\n- Check import paths work correctly\n- Ensure backward compatibility\n\n## Rollback Strategy\nIf any optimizer breaks:\n- Revert that specific optimizer file to original\n- Investigate root cause in shared helper\n- Fix helper function\n- Re-attempt update\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":9,"cache_creation_input_tokens":204,"cache_read_input_tokens":61194,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":204},"output_tokens":2,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"3e0addbe-3a14-4b81-856f-09cdbc90aa87","uuid":"e518f4af-43f6-4619-921f-f9465c8aab44"}

These 11+ optimizer files currently duplicate substantial amounts of common infrastructure code, making maintenance difficult and preventing consistent improvements.\n\nThe goal is to extract repeated patterns into a shared `torch/optim/_foreach.py` module while maintaining 100% backward compatibility with public APIs.\n\n## Problem Statement\n**Current state:** 11 optimizer files each contain a `_multi_tensor_*` function with 200-400+ lines of code\n- Step counter updates (CPU optimization) - Applies the CPU-specific step update optimization\n   - Avoids repeated torch.tensor() allocations\n   - Used in: Adam, Adamax, Adadelta, ASGD, RMSprop, Rprop, NAdam, RAdam (8+ files)\n\n3. **`_apply_complex_view_if_needed(has_complex, params, grads, *state_tensors)`**\n   - Converts complex tensors to real view for processing\n   - Used in: Adam, Adagrad, Adamax, Adadelta, ASGD, RMSprop, Rprop, NAdam (7+ files)\n\n4. **`_handle_capturable_bias_correction(betas, state_steps, lr, capturable, is_compiling)`**\n   - Unified capturable vs non-capturable bias correction logic\n   - Returns appropriate tensor or list of scalars\n   - Used in: Adam, Adamax, Adadelta, ASGD, RMSprop, Rprop, NAdam\n\n5. **`_validate_foreach_inputs(params, grad_scale, found_inf, differentiable, function_name)`**\n   -
