These 11+ optimizer files currently duplicate substantial amounts of common infrastructure code, making maintenance difficult and preventing consistent improvements.\n\nThe goal is to extract repeated patterns into a shared `torch/optim/_foreach.py` module while maintaining 100% backward compatibility with public APIs.\n\n## Problem Statement\n**Current state:** 11 optimizer files each contain a `_multi_tensor_*` function with 200-400+ lines of code\n- Step counter updates (CPU optimization) - duplicated 8+ times\n- Weight decay + maximize pattern - duplicated 7+ times\n- Complex number conversion - duplicated 7+ times\n- Device/dtype grouping + casting - duplicated in every file\n- Sparse gradient checks - several files\n\nThis duplication makes it difficult to:\n- Fix bugs consistently across all optimizers\n- Add features (e.g., AMP support) to all optimizers uniformly\n- Understand the core algorithm vs infrastructure code\n\n## Solution Overview\nCreate a new `torch/optim/_foreach.py` module with reusable helper functions extracted from the common patterns identified across all `_multi_tensor_*` implementations.\n\n### Key Design Principles\n1. **Don't over-engineer**: Only extract code that is actually duplicated across 2+ optimizers\n2. **Keep algorithm-specific logic in optimizer files**: Each optimizer's core algorithm stays in its file\n3. **Focus on infrastructure**: Extract device/dtype grouping, step updates, complex handling, maximize, weight decay utilities\n4. **Backward compatibility**: All public APIs remain unchanged; this is purely internal refactoring\n5. **Minimal dependencies**: New module should depend only on torch and optimizer.py utilities\n\n## Implementation Plan\n\n### Phase 1: Create `torch/optim/_foreach.py` Module\nCreate new file with shared helper functions based on duplicated patterns:\n\n**File: `/workspace/torch/optim/_foreach.py`**\n\nFunctions to extract (in priority order of duplication):\n\n1. **`_apply_weight_decay_and_maximize(grads, params, weight_decay, maximize)`**\n   - Combines the maximize negation + weight decay application pattern\n   - Handles memory reuse when both operations are needed\n   - Used in: SGD, Adam, Adagrad, Adamax, Adadelta, ASGD, RMSprop (7+ files)\n\n2. **`_update_step_counters(state_steps, is_compiling)`**\n   - Applies the CPU-specific step update optimization\n   - Avoids repeated torch.tensor() allocations\n   - Used in: Adam, Adamax, Adadelta, ASGD, RMSprop, Rprop, NAdam, RAdam (8+ files)\n\n3. **`_apply_complex_view_if_needed(has_complex, params, grads, *state_tensors)`**\n   - Converts complex tensors to real view for processing\n   - Used in: Adam, Adagrad, Adamax, Adadelta, ASGD, RMSprop, Rprop, NAdam (7+ files)\n\n4. **`_handle_capturable_bias_correction(betas, state_steps, lr, capturable, is_compiling)`**\n   - Unified capturable vs non-capturable bias correction logic\n   - Returns appropriate tensor or list of scalars\n   - Used in: Adam, Adamax, Adadelta, ASGD, RMSprop, Rprop, NAdam\n\n5. **`_validate_foreach_inputs(params, grad_scale, found_inf, differentiable, function_name)`**\n   - Centralize validation logic for foreach operations\n   - Check empty params, AMP assertions, etc.\n\n### Phase 2: Update Optimizer Files (Priority Order)\nUpdate the following files to import and use helpers from `_foreach.py`:\n\n1. **`torch/optim/sgd.py`** (_multi_tensor_sgd)\n   - Replace weight_decay + maximize logic with shared function\n   - Straightforward refactoring - minimal algorithm complexity\n\n2. **`torch/optim/adam.py`** (_multi_tensor_adam)\n   - Replace weight_decay + maximize logic\n   - Replace step update logic\n   - Replace complex number handling\n   - Keep bias correction logic (may share later)\n\n3. **`torch/optim/adamax.py`** (_multi_tensor_adamax)\n   - Same pattern as Adam\n\n4. **`torch/optim/rmsprop.py`** (_multi_tensor_rmsprop)\n   - Replace step update logic\n   - Replace complex number handling\n   - Replace weight_decay + maximize logic\n\n5. **`torch/optim/adadelta.py`** (_multi_tensor_adadelta)\n   - Similar to RMSprop pattern\n\n6. **`torch/optim/adagrad.py`** (_multi_tensor_adagrad)\n   - Has sparse handling - needs careful refactoring\n\n7. Others as time permits (ASGD, NAdam, RAdam, Rprop, Radadelta if needed)\n\n### Phase 3: Testing Strategy\n1. **Compile test** - Ensure no import/syntax errors\n2. **Run existing optimizer tests** - All should pass unchanged\n   - `python -m pytest test/test_optim.py -v` (or equivalent)\n3. **Numerical equivalence** - Foreach results vs single-tensor should match\n4. **Edge cases** - Empty params, single param, multi-device, etc.\n\n## Critical Implementation Details\n\n### Signature Patterns (Do NOT break)\nAll functions must maintain existing signatures - no changes to public optimizer APIs:\n- `sgd(params, d_p_list, momentum_buffer_list, ..., foreach=None, ...)`\n- `adam(params, grads, exp_avgs, ..., foreach=None, ...)`\n- All dispatch logic stays in optimizer files\n\n### What Stays in Optimizer Files\n- Dispatcher functions (sgd, adam, etc.) that choose single_tensor vs multi_tensor vs fused\n- Optimizer class definitions and state management\n- Algorithm-specific logic that's unique to each optimizer\n- Public docstrings and examples\n\n### What Moves to `_foreach.py`\n- Utility functions for common operations\n- Grouping/casting infrastructure\n- Step counter updates\n- Maximize + weight decay utilities\n- Complex number handling helpers\n- Validation helpers\n\n## Files to Modify\n1. **Create:** `/workspace/torch/optim/_foreach.py` (NEW)\n2. **Update:** `/workspace/torch/optim/sgd.py`\n3. **Update:** `/workspace/torch/optim/adam.py`\n4. **Update:** `/workspace/torch/optim/adamax.py`\n5. **Update:** `/workspace/torch/optim/rmsprop.py`\n6. **Update:** `/workspace/torch/optim/adadelta.py`\n7. **Update:** `/workspace/torch/optim/adagrad.py`\n8. *Others as time permits*\n\n## Success Criteria\n- [ ] `_foreach.py` module created with helper functions\n- [ ] At least 3 optimizer files (SGD, Adam, RMSprop) updated to use shared helpers\n- [ ] All existing tests pass without modification\n- [ ] Numerical equivalence verified (single-tensor vs multi-tensor outputs match)\n- [ ] Code duplication reduced by 30%+ across updated files\n- [ ] No changes to public APIs or behavior\n\n## Implementation Order\n1.
